SENTIENT SPECIES:
Slim Dwarfoids: Fond of drink and industry - especially building strange contraptions. They have bilateral symmetry and a slim shape. They are peaceful and have a complex system of social rules. They first evolved on Taranis III in 650.
	Their Stats are: STR: 1 DEX: 0 CON: 0 INT: 1 CHA: 2
Telepathic Catoids: Always curious and often cruel. They have bilateral symmetry. They can read each others' minds. They are cowardly and have a complex system of social rules. They were uplifted by the Republic of Robots, Catoids, Deep Dwellers, Koboldoids and Ursoids on Genur VI in 900.
	Their Stats are: STR: 1 DEX: -1 CON: -1 INT: 1 CHA: -1
Orange Deep Dwellers: They live in the deep oceans or in deep caves, hiding. Their presence can go unnoticed for a long time. They have orange skin. They have bilateral symmetry. They are hyperactive and deeply rationalist. They first evolved on Erebus V in 930.
	Their Stats are: STR: 2 DEX: -2 CON: -1 INT: 0 CHA: 1
Four-Armed Humanoids: Pretty adventurous but otherwise fairly average. They have four arms. They have bilateral symmetry. They are cowardly and strive to uphold their ideals of personal honour. They first evolved on Cykov I in 822.
	Their Stats are: STR: 2 DEX: 2 CON: -1 INT: -1 CHA: 1
Green Dwarfoids: Fond of drink and industry - especially building strange contraptions. They have green skin. They have bilateral symmetry. They are cowardly and believe in the survival of the fittest. They first evolved on Erebus V in 926.
	Their Stats are: STR: 1 DEX: -3 CON: 3 INT: 1 CHA: 0
Flying Yellow Ursoids with Long Tails: Always at war with someone, or everyone, or one another. They have yellow skin. They have bilateral symmetry. They use their long tails for balance. They can fly. They are reclusive and have a complex system of social castes. They first evolved on Hylon VI in 962.
	Their Stats are: STR: -1 DEX: -1 CON: 0 INT: -1 CHA: 2
Giant Deep Dwellers: They live in the deep oceans or in deep caves, hiding. Their presence can go unnoticed for a long time. They have bilateral symmetry. They are fond of practical jokes and have a complex system of social castes. They first evolved on Taranis III in 887.
	Their Stats are: STR: 1 DEX: 0 CON: -1 INT: 1 CHA: -1
Scaly Humanoids: Pretty adventurous but otherwise fairly average. They have bilateral symmetry. They are peaceful and value personal integrity above all else. They first evolved on Hylon VI in 960.
	Their Stats are: STR: -2 DEX: 0 CON: 1 INT: 1 CHA: -2
Yellow Trolloids: They have lost the ability to reproduce naturally, and compensate for this with a focus on science and paranoia. They have yellow skin. They have bilateral symmetry. They are hyperactive and unwilling to compromise. They first evolved on Sativex III in 939.
	Their Stats are: STR: 1 DEX: -3 CON: 0 INT: 1 CHA: -1
Two-Headed Yellow Robots: Purely mechanical lifeforms, artificially created. They have yellow skin. They have two heads that tend to constantly bicker with one another. They have bilateral symmetry. They are peaceful and deeply rationalist. They were created by the Republic of Antoids, Robots and Deep Dwellers on Atria IV as servants in 630.
	Their Stats are: STR: 0 DEX: -1 CON: 1 INT: 1 CHA: 2
Telepathic Humanoids with Threefold Symmetry: Pretty adventurous but otherwise fairly average. They have trilateral symmetry. They can read each others' minds. They are cowardly and deeply rationalist. They first evolved on Golet I in 876.
	Their Stats are: STR: 1 DEX: 2 CON: 0 INT: 1 CHA: 1
Scaly Green Ursoids: Always at war with someone, or everyone, or one another. They have green scales. They have bilateral symmetry. They are thrill-seeking and have a complex system of social castes. They first evolved on Genur VI in 787.
	Their Stats are: STR: -1 DEX: -1 CON: 1 INT: -1 CHA: -1
Six-Legged Robots with Long Tails: Purely mechanical lifeforms, artificially created. They have six legs. They have bilateral symmetry. They use their long tails for balance. They are fond of practical jokes and believe in the inherent superiority of their species. They were created by the Kingdom of Robots, Dwarfoids, Catoids, Deep Dwellers, Humanoids, Koboldoids, Trolloids and Ursoids on Jurvox I as servants in 1008.
	Their Stats are: STR: 0 DEX: 1 CON: 1 INT: 1 CHA: -1
Slim Koboldoids: Eat pretty much anything, including one another. Disturbingly fond of skulls. They have bilateral symmetry and a slim shape. They are reclusive and strive to uphold their ideals of personal honour. They first evolved on Sativex III in 943.
	Their Stats are: STR: -1 DEX: 0 CON: 2 INT: 1 CHA: 1
Telepathic Koboldoids with Long Tails: Eat pretty much anything, including one another. Disturbingly fond of skulls. They have bilateral symmetry. They use their long tails for balance. They can read each others' minds. They are humorless and deeply religious. They first evolved on Hylon VI in 777.
	Their Stats are: STR: -1 DEX: 0 CON: 2 INT: 0 CHA: 2
Telepathic Purple Robots with Threefold Symmetry: Purely mechanical lifeforms, artificially created. They have purple skin. They have trilateral symmetry. They can read each others' minds. They are humorless and strive to uphold their ideals of personal honour. They were created by the Republic of Antoids and Robots on Golet I as servants in 520.
	Their Stats are: STR: -2 DEX: 1 CON: 0 INT: 1 CHA: 0

CIVILISATIONS:
THE EMPIRE OF GREEN DWARFOIDS:
An ancient, corrupt, fantastically wealthy, highly advanced Empire of 5 planets, with 100 billion inhabitants.
Major populations:
8 billion Green Dwarfoids.
13 billion enslaved Slim Dwarfoids.
5 billion enslaved Scaly Green Ursoids.
5 billion enslaved Telepathic Catoids.
12 billion enslaved Four-Armed Humanoids.
5 billion enslaved Telepathic Koboldoids with Long Tails.
4 billion enslaved Giant Deep Dwellers.
21 billion enslaved Telepathic Purple Robots with Threefold Symmetry.
11 billion enslaved Telepathic Humanoids with Threefold Symmetry.
16 billion enslaved Two-Headed Yellow Robots.
It controls a Teleport Gate.
It is at war with the Kingdom of Robots, Dwarfoids, Catoids, Deep Dwellers, Humanoids, Koboldoids, Trolloids and Ursoids.

	Their Stats are: STR: 0 DEX: -2 CON: 0 INT: 0 CHA: 0
THE KINGDOM OF ROBOTS, DWARFOIDS, CATOIDS, DEEP DWELLERS, HUMANOIDS, KOBOLDOIDS, TROLLOIDS AND URSOIDS:
A well-established, fantastically wealthy, highly advanced Kingdom of 12 planets, with 97 billion inhabitants.
Major populations:
3 billion Telepathic Catoids.
10 billion Orange Deep Dwellers.
8 billion Four-Armed Humanoids.
9 billion Green Dwarfoids.
6 billion Scaly Humanoids.
7 billion Yellow Trolloids.
22 billion Two-Headed Yellow Robots.
10 billion Scaly Green Ursoids.
3 billion Telepathic Koboldoids with Long Tails.
7 billion Telepathic Purple Robots with Threefold Symmetry.
3 billion enslaved Flying Yellow Ursoids with Long Tails.
2 billion enslaved Six-Legged Robots with Long Tails.
7 billion enslaved Slim Koboldoids.
It controls a Universal Antidote.
It is at war with the Empire of Green Dwarfoids.

	Their Stats are: STR: 1 DEX: -1 CON: 1 INT: 1 CHA: 1
PLANETS:

Shape-shifters: A predatory creature able to mimic any other, even a sentient one.

Pharmaceuticals: Plants that contain interesting chemical compounds with medical applications.

Ocean giants: Huge sea creatures growing to more than a kilometre of length.

XARLAN IV
A barren planet of the Kingdom of Robots, Dwarfoids, Catoids, Deep Dwellers, Humanoids, Koboldoids, Trolloids and Ursoids.
In orbit: The pirate Greenbeard, a Four-Armed Humanoids, commanding a fleet of 7 ships.
A military base, built by the Kingdom of Robots, Dwarfoids, Catoids, Deep Dwellers, Humanoids, Koboldoids, Trolloids and Ursoids in 1006
Titanic Mountains: Mountain ranges so vast they poke out of the atmosphere into space.

The Empire of Green Dwarfoids attack Sativex III, a colony of the Kingdom of Robots, Dwarfoids, Catoids, Deep Dwellers, Humanoids, Koboldoids, Trolloids and Ursoids, and subject it to orbital bombardment, killing 12 billion.

The Kingdom of Robots, Dwarfoids, Catoids, Deep Dwellers, Humanoids, Koboldoids, Trolloids and Ursoids conquer Hylon VI, a colony of the Empire of Green Dwarfoids, killing 1 billion in the process.
The pirate Greenbeard receives tribute from Xarlan IV of the Kingdom of Robots, Dwarfoids, Catoids, Deep Dwellers, Humanoids, Koboldoids, Trolloids and Ursoids.
